3.1.2.3 
Encrypted clients 
Datahub enables the so-called going through the processes of "encrypted" customers. With an encrypted client 
means that the customer has been granted a restraining order or has himself refused 
transfer of his data and his data may not be forwarded. You can apply for a security ban 
from the registrar, if the person has a justified reason to doubt his or his family's safety 
at hazard. Encrypted customer does not mean a customer who has informed the party of the ban 
from transfer for direct marketing purposes. If there is an entry in the customer's information 
regarding the confidentiality of customer data, the information is forwarded in the normal way in contract processes 
from the seller to the distribution system operator. Information about confidentiality goes to the new contract 
along with the customer information attached to the notification, also to the information of the distribution system operator. Encrypted 
marked customers cannot give authorizations to 3rd parties. If the customer who is notified 
"encrypted" information, is the authorization given by the 3rd party at the time of notification, the authorization ends 
as a matter of routine. The information about the customer becoming encrypted is forwarded to the customer data 
according to the update event, to the customer's other sellers and distribution system operators normally. 
However, distribution system operators and sellers can forward these customers' data to datahub 
through in those situations where these market parties authorize 3rd parties to act 
in turn. However, the 3rd parties may not use the customer's information in these situations 
to anything other than what is agreed with the market party in the role of the market party 
to a working process. If the customer wants to remove the "encrypted" mark from his data, it is up to the customer 
change this information yourself in the datahub customer portal.

to contract processes. Consequently, a search functionality will be built into the data hub, which 
returns the data of the place of use, the data of the customers connected to the place of use with contracts, and the data 
in accordance with the rights of the requesting party regarding the contractual situation of the place of use. Search returns information

about the obligation to correct the customer's invoicing and the final invoice of the Electricity Market Act 
of the dispatch requirement in accordance with the current operating method. This 6 week contract 
from the end, the seller is called the "outgoing seller" in datahub's processes.  
In contrast to the previous one, with the customer's authorization, the seller can apply for a customer and user location 
information even without a valid contract. The principles of authorizations are described in more detail 
in chapter 3.9. 
Distribution system operators have rights to the usage location data of their own measurement areas, and therefore also 
to the customer data connected to these places of use with an online contract. Made by the distribution system operator 
the search for usage location information always returns the customer and 
online contract information if there is a customer at the point of use. 
3.1.4 
DH-140 Maintenance of energy community information 
On 22 December 2020, the State Council approved the report on electricity supplies andgiven from the measurement 
amendment of the government decree. Provisions on local were added to the regulation 
about the energy community and the group of active customers and their tasks. Coming into force 
in accordance with the regulation, the datahub deals with local energy communities and active customers 
group-related processes from the beginning of 2023. Both the energy community and the active ones 
the information of the customer group is maintained using the same energy community processes described below. 
Energy community information in the data hub can be maintained by the distribution network operator in the measurement area 
the energy community in question is.  
In accordance with the regulation, the energy community is notified to the distribution system operator 14 days before the community 
start of calculations. The distribution system operator must report the information to datahub no later than 7 days before 
the start of calculations. Energy community information can be reported by the community for 90 days at the earliest 
entry into force.  
The energy community is identified in the data hub with the party's own identifier. The identifier is generated 
such as the customer's own identifier (distribution system operator's GLN code + distribution system operator 
ID provided). The community identifier must be unique. In addition to the identifier, the distribution system operator 
enter the name of the community in datahub.

SMA, chapter 3.3.8.1). This information is given when the community is created.  
If the allocation of the surplus is done per place of use (SMB), it will go to each community 
the consuming use place is connected to the small production use place, to which the surplus is allocated. If 
the consumption location is not associated with a (real) production location, the distribution system operator must create a so-called 
virtual place of use. The distribution system operator must create this virtual 
small production use place before establishing community data. For these virtual ones 
similar sales and network agreements must be made for small production locations as for normal ones 
for small production use. In the SMB sharing method, the energy community must also be assigned a separate one 
surplus production utilization site, to which the surpluses of any cut off are allocated 
in terms of places of use.  
If the surplus is allocated to only one Community Production Use Site (SMA), this will be the case 
the place of use specifies the surplus place of use for community information.  
Notification of a new energy community must also be made if the energy community's surplus distribution method 
changes (the distribution method cannot be changed with an update event). In this case, the decision is made using the old method of distribution 
existing energy community and a new energy community with a new distribution method is announced. This should be taken into account 
time limits in the notification of a new entity.   
With the update event, you can change the places of use belonging to the community. It is also in the update 
it should be noted that the distribution shares of the places of use must always be 100% in total and that the individual 
the distribution share of the place of use cannot be 100%. The distribution system operator must notify 
on the update of the energy community information no later than 7 days before the effective date of the change. 
The change can be made no earlier than 90 days before the effective date of the change.  
When the energy community decides its operations, the distribution system operator must also decide on the information 
from datahub. Termination is subject to the same time limits as updating community information, i.e 
termination must be notified at least 7 days before the end of the community. Closing event 
delete information about the energy community from the place of use belonging to the community on the date announced.  
Datahub informs the current vendor of the usage location as well as a possible oneto an authorized party 
information about the updating of the usage location information when the usage location is either added as a new one 
to the energy community or is removed from the energy community by updating or terminating the community.

3.2 
DH-300 Contract processes 
This chapter describes the processes related to point of use sales and online contracts. 
In principle, every time the seller makes a new contract in his own system, a notification is given 
from there to datahub. The distribution system operator confirms its own contract, if necessary 
to datahub always based on the seller's notification. If the seller or the distribution network operator makes changes 
to the contract information stored in the datahub, the changes are reported to the datahub and the datahub forwards them 
to the other party. At the end of the contract, both parties terminate their own contracts, and done 
the termination of the contract is communicated to the other party via datahub.  It cannot be at the place of use 
valid at the same time as one sales contract and one network contract, so datahub decides 
automatically of the previous contract when the place of use is notified of a new contract, and 
convey information about the terminated contract to the party whose contract was terminated. 
3.2.1 
Contract information 
The sales and network contract information stored in Datahub includes, among other things, the contract 
dates, billing address and contact information. When the parties announce the concluded 
contracts with datahub, the customer information provided in the notification is stored in datahub's Customer
to the entity (or to several, if the contract has more than one customer), and the contract 
is connected to the Customer (or customers) and to the notified in the data hub's internal data structure 
To the place of use. If the reported customer is still not found in the data hub, a new one is created in the data hub 
customer. In the case of a customer already found in the data hub, the customer's information is updated with the new one 
in connection with the announcement of the contract. Any changed customer information will be forwarded to everyone 
for parties who are entitled to customer data (see section 3.1.2.2 Correctness of customer data 
and maintenance) An individual contract is identified in datahub by the contract ID, 
with a combination of the location ID and the ID of the market party related to the contract. 
Contracts entered in Datahub are valid for whole days. The contract 
the start date is the first day the contract is valid. The contract 
the end date is the first day on which the contract is no longer valid. That's the deal 
starts at 00:00 on the effective date stated in the agreement notification. The contract ends again 
as the end date of the termination notice at 00:00, i.e. the day before the end date 
is the last day the contract is valid.  
Information about the invoicing channel is stored in the contract data, and according to this, the contract data will be entered 
attach the invoicing address information according to the desired invoicing channel (including invoicing (postal) address, 
email invoice address or online invoice address). A new contract for the customer's seller 
the invoicing address provided at the time of signing is forwarded from the seller via datahub 
to the distribution system operator. However, this information does not bind the distribution system operator to use the 
billing channel if this channel is not available. The distribution system operator informs the data hub 
information of the billing channel used in the contract as part of the online contract. The customer can too 
want the distribution network operator to send invoices to a different address than the sales invoice. Here 
the customer must contact the distribution system operator to change the billing address. 
The distribution system operator informs the data hub of the billing address change. Datahub's data model 
enables the use of separate billing addresses for the sales and

invoicing method of their contract. 
Contracts can include contact persons in addition to the actual customer. The customer is real 
contractual partner who is legally responsible for the contract. The contact persons are related to the contract 
persons whose contact information the parties need in customer service situations. For example, an invoice 
the recipient can be indicated as the contract's contact person, if it is different from the actual customer.  
Likewise, the contract contact persons may differ between sales and online contracts. To the customer 
the contact person's information provided to the seller in connection with the conclusion of a new contract 
is stored in the sales contract data, and forwarded to the distribution system operator. The distribution system operator can 
use these as contact persons for their own contract. It should be noted that the parties may have 
many different types of contact persons in their own customer and contract information, but to datahub 
the contact persons whose information needs to be passed on between the parties are indicated. 
Business customers must be notified of at least one contact person. Personal customers will be notified separately 
contact person only as needed, if the customer's contact information is not sufficient.  
The contract must state the way of doing business agreed with the customer. Transaction method "electronic" 
primarily means that no letter is sent to the customer. The way of doing business is contract-specific and 
the transaction method agreed by the seller with the customer is also forwarded to the distribution system operator for information. 
However, the distribution system operator must always agree on an electronic way of doing business with the customer 
separately, even though the seller has declared himself to be using an electronic transaction method. If for the contract 
the chosen transaction method is electronic, at least one of the customers connected to the contract must have one 
email address in contact information.

the online contract can be valid at the same time. The contractual information transmitted in the processes is

reporting to datahub is always initiated by the seller. However, this does not prevent the distribution system operator 
of the agreed online contract with the customer before the customer has signed 
sales contract with the seller. If the distribution network operator enters into a network contract before 
a new sales contract has been notified to datahub, the distribution system operator must wait for a new one 
notification of the sales contract from the datahub, and confirms the online contract to the datahub only after this 
after according to the normal process.

3.2.2.1 
Creation of an online contract 
Datahub infers the information of the seller's announcement and the place of use from its current customer and 
about the contract situation, whether a new network contract is needed. When it comes to moving in, let's do it 
new online contract always. When it comes to a change of vendor or contract, a new one is needed 
network agreement in those situations where the valid network agreement of the place of use is different 
with the customer as a future sales contract. This practice ensures that in the future the place of use 
sales and online contracts will be concluded for the same customers. Although customers with contracts 
would be the same, a new online contract is also needed if the new online contract is about to expire 
during the sales contract, or if the online contract is pending cancellation notified by the seller 
based on the cancellation of the sales contract. A new online contract is also required if the contracts 
The "electricity supply agreement" fields do not match each other. The field in question will be checked again 
between and existing sales contract or, if no previous sales contract is valid, 
but a valid online contract is found, the review is done for a new sales contract and 
between an existing network contract. If a new network contract is not needed, don't care 
datahub for the distribution system operator, however, information about the new sales contract. In this situation 
the seller gets the necessary information about the location of use and e.g. network agreement of the place of use 
after the product information sales contract comes into force, location of use and customer information 
at the application event.  
If a new online contract is needed, datahub creates a new one based on the seller's notification 
network contract information to the status "unconfirmed". Datahub sends a notification to the distribution system operator 
of the new network contract, which the distribution system operator confirms to the data hub with its own 
with his notification. An unconfirmed contract from Datahub is formed 
in the datahub, own contract ID, which the distribution system operator must replace in its own system 
with the existing contract code. The distribution system operator may have entered into an agreement earlier 
with the customer, in which case the details of the contract are sent as confirmation at this stage 
to datahub. Information about the distribution system operator's confirmation is also forwarded to the seller, in which case the seller receives 
information necessary for their knowledge of the online agreement, such as product information.  
If necessary, the distribution system operator will connect the electricity to the place of use on the day of the start of delivery. The seller does not 
need to send a separate connection request, the distribution network operator will connect the electricity again 
based on the contract notification. The connection is announced with the connection notification according to chapter 3.4. 
If the distribution system operator cannot connect electricity to the place of use when the contract starts, this will notify 
regarding this to the seller outside the datahub. In the contract information forwarded to the distribution system operator, 
the seller will provide information on whether the place of use is critical for interruption upon signing the contract 
due to the special needs of the customer and/or the resident living at the place of use. Interrupt critical 
the point of use should not be disconnected under normal circumstances, but that information does not guide how 
the distribution network operator controls the power cut at the point of use, for example, if possible 
in the event of a power shortage.

3.2.2.3 
Code 
In Datahub, the contract start date refers to the day from which the seller has 
the right to measurement data and from when the seller is responsible for the consumption or production of the place of use 
in its own balance sheet. In practice, this date also corresponds to the day from which 
the seller has the right to invoice the customer.  
In the current situation, a lot of investigation work is causing the same place of use for the same or close ones 
new sales contract announcements made for the dates. It will be clear in Datahub 
the rules, under what conditions and for what period of time new sales contracts can be announced for the place of use. 
The main principle is that two or more cannot be valid on the same date at the same time 
sales contract at the same place of use. The contracts are always valid for full days, i.e 
the agreement enters into force on the day it starts at 00:00 and the agreement ends at the end of the day.  
The rules for notifications to the same place of use are as follows: 
1. A new sales contract can be announced as starting on the current day whenever the place of use is 
without a seller 
2. Moving in must be announced no later than the current day and no earlier than 90 days 
before the start date of the contract. 
3. In situations of contract exchange (see tablekko 9) a new sales contract can be announced 
to start for the current day. 
4. In situations other than the three above, a new sales contract must be notified 
at least 14 days later and no earlier than 90 days before the contract 
start date. 
5. A new sales contract that has been successfully notified to datahub is automatically terminated 
the new sales contract of the sales contract valid on the starting date 
for the day before the start date (also applies to situations where the previous customer is 
reported moving out to a later date when the end date 
will be updated to earlier). 
6. At the place of use, containing temporary or different terms of termination 
according to its validity, the sales contract prevents new ones announced by the new seller 
sales contracts where the customer or one of the customers is the same as the place of use 
in the valid sales contract.

3.2.2.5 
Fixed-term sales agreements 
The fixed-term nature of a sales agreement is reported to Datahub by notifying such an agreement of the 
start date of the fixed-term and the end date of the fixed-term. It should be noted that 
in the Datahub data model, these are different information than the start and 
end dates of the agreement. The start date of the agreement is always the correct start time of the agreement. 
The end date of the agreement is only saved when the termination of the agreement is reported to Datahub or Datahub terminates the agreement automatically. 
The fixed-term nature of sales contracts will be taken into account in Datahub using the same principles as in the current model. The main rule is that a fixed-term contract can be terminated early if the customer moves away from the location of use. In Datahub, contracts are always examined on a site-by-site basis, so even if the seller and the customer have agreed to continue the fixed-term contract at the customer's new location of use, from Datahub's perspective these are two different contracts for different locations of use, in which case the first contract can be terminated in Datahub. 
In Datahub, a fixed-term contract prevents a new seller from concluding a new sales contract in a situation where even one customer in the current sales contract at the location of use is the same as the contracting parties to the new sales contract (cases 4 and 5 in Table 7 of Chapter 3.2.2). 
The customer can agree on contract changes and new contract terms with their current seller flexibly. Therefore, the customer can agree to remove and add parties to their contract, for example in the event of a separation with their current vendor, even if the customer's current contract is for a fixed term. However, the fixed term of the current contract prevents the notification of a new vendor's contract to Datahub. The fixed term of the contract does not prevent the vendor from terminating the sales contract with a separate termination notification. 
The following table summarizes the deadlines for notifying contracts to Datahub in different situations, the effect of the fixed term, and the reason for notifying a new contract registered by Datahub.

Rules for processing fixed-term contracts in Datahub: 
1. A fixed-term sales contract is deemed to continue to be valid until further notice if the termination of the contract or the renewal of the fixed-term contract is not separately 
notified to Datahub. 
2. A new seller may notify a consumer customer who has a fixed-term sales contract of a new 
sales contract if the fixed-term nature of the contract has continued for at least 2 years. 
3. If the current seller wishes to terminate the current fixed-term contract and continue the 
contract with a new one for at leastwhile some of the current customers remain the same, new ones 
the contract can be reported directly to datahub.  
4. The renewal of the fixed term is announced with the contract update event (chapter 3.2.3), 
to which the seller indicates the start and end dates of the new term which 
will come into force at the time the change enters into force.

3.2.2.6 
Different terms of termination 
The seller can agree on different terms of termination for non-consumer customers in the contract. 
According to the data model described earlier, the sales contract has information about whether the contract contains 
different terms of termination. In contracts where the customer's notice period is longer than usual (14 
days) is different, the seller must notify this different notice period. In others 
in the information on unusual notice terms, either the length of the unusual notice period must be stated 
days, or a date range within which a new sales contract can be started. If necessary, the seller 
must report updated information in these respects every day.  
For example, if the seller has a contract that can be terminated on the 5th of every month, the seller must 
continuously update the information to reflect the next possible day according to the notice period, 
when a new sales contract can be started. The indicated date (or date range) will 
to state the day or time when the new sales contract can be started, and not the day when 
the customer has the right to terminate the contract. If the seller states the date range is the first 
the indicated day is the day when the new contract can start and the last day is the day when it can no longer be 
start a new contract. In the case of the example, a specific single day can be reported 
as a date range, where the end date is the day after the start date.  
According to its rules, a deviating termination clause in the contract prevents a new sales contract 
making to the customer's current place of use corresponding to the current place of use 
fixed-term sales contract. The new seller will be notified of the unusual termination condition 
the start date of the first possible contract, even when this is more than 90 days 
off. However, even in this case, the contract cannot be notified for more than 90 days 
on.   
3.2.3 
DH-320 Notification of contract changes 
Whenever a party makes changes in its own system to the data stored in the data hub, 
changes must be reported to datahub. When updating the contract, the contract to be updated is identified 
by means of a combination of contract ID, market party and usage location ID. For contracts 
the changes to be made are reported to datahub according to the following rules: 
1. You cannot add or remove customers to the contract with an update event, but in this case there will be 
announces a new sales contract. The contract's customer information cannot be updated either 
with contract update. Updating the customer's information is described in chapter 3.1.2. 
2. By updating the contract, the start or end time of the contract cannot be changed. To Datahub 
the start or end dates of the sales contract can be changed before these 
dates (i.e. not retroactively) only in such a way that the original is reported to datahub first 
cancellation of the notification and then a new notification with a new date. 
3. Change of the start and end dates of the sales contract after the delivery has started or already 
after completion is described in chapter 3.2.5.

DH-330 Notice of Termination of Contracts 
As described above, the notification of the new sales contract terminates the previous one of the place of use 
the contract automatically changes the start date of the new contract to the previous day. In addition to this 
it is possible to notify datahub separately of the termination of contracts. In these cases 
the main principle is that the notification that terminates the contract in datahub, i.e. records the contract 
the end date is always done by the party whose contract ends. Datahub sends 
of the termination of the contract to the notification to the other party, who decides (his own process 
in accordance with) his own agreement in his own system, and informs about this on his own 
with a notice of termination to datahub. Datahub can, however, terminate the customer's contract 
via the seller also informs the customer of the new place of use, in which case the termination notice is forwarded 
to the distribution system operator of the place of use. In this case, the distribution system operator must do the actual work 
ending the contract with the data hub, as you would do in a situation where the customer announces they are moving out 
to the distribution system operator directly.

from the data hub to the distribution network operator of the relocation destination. The distribution system operator of the emigration destination

in a situation where the customer would have notified the distribution network operator of the move out. This process 
with this, the notification of the termination of the contract is then forwarded from the data hub to the relocation destination 
to the seller. The seller of the move-in property must provide at least one customer who has 
contract at the move-out destination, identification information for notification. In order to notify the customer 
moving out to datahub, the seller must first inform datahub of the customer's new sales contract.

the seller has not announced all the customers of the contract. Separate from the seller of the move-in property 
the move-out notification cannot be canceled in datahub. If the seller discovers that he has sent a notice 
incorrectly, the seller must be in direct contact with the relevant distribution system operator.

there is no old seller at the place of use to whom the contract is returned, corresponds to the disputed contract 
seller from the balance sheets until a new seller or distribution system operator appears at the place of use 
cuts off the electricity.

the repair processes performed by the operator to the contract data are described.  
3.2.4.5 
DH-323 Vendor-free places of use 
So that the distribution network operator can, if he wishes, terminate his own network contract and/or cut off the electricity 
from the point of use, datahub sends notifications of points of use without vendors to the distribution system operator. 
Notifications of locations without vendors are sent daily. The notification will indicate when 
the place of use remained or is about to remain without a seller, and when the seller-free period is ending, if 
datahub has a sales contract that will start at a later date for the place of use. Datahub sends 
announcements about even short periods without sellers.  
It should be noted, however, that datahub does not send notifications about places of use that are in data conversion 
are brought connected and without a seller.

in distance selling situations and to correct incorrect contracts. General principle with cancellation 
is that the contract is canceled from the start date of the contract. Based on the reason for cancellation is 
however, there are some exceptions to the situation, which will be opened in later examples. The real ones

the seller has the right to data about the place of use (including measurement data) in datahub. Contract information 
corresponds to the time from which the seller has the right to bill the customer. Under normal circumstances, balance sheet information 
corresponds to contract information. The balance sheet information may differ from the contractual information when retroactive corrections are made. 
3.2.5.1 
Cancellation of the sales contract 
Sales contracts are canceled when the customer cancels the contract using the statutory provisions 
right of cancellation or in error situations where there is a sales contract or possibly an online contract 
made for the wrong place of use or otherwise on the wrong grounds. Cancellation can be made before 
the beginning of the contract or retroactively after the beginning of the contract. These two cases 
the cancellation process is handled differently in datahub. 
The seller must notify datahub of the cancellation of the contract. Can be canceled in most situations 
the sales contract was originally decided by the previous seller of the place of use when it was announced 
of the sales contract, in which case this will be reinstated upon cancellation. No refunds will be made 
for a contract that has been concluded with a separate termination event (seller's own notification or 
mass termination of contracts by the operator). It has been agreed in the industry that the previous seller should 
take the customer back into his sales, unless it is a fixed-term contract of the customer, which is already in place 
finished. If the seller of the previous contract does not want the customer back, the latter can refuse 
on the return of the contract (transaction DH-343). Refusal to return the contract is responsible 
termination of the contract and it always uses termination as the reason for the termination of the contract. If 
the seller of the previous contract wants to end the contract with something else after the cancellation 
with the reason for termination, the termination is announced as a normal termination of the contract with the event DH-
331. In moving-in situations, there is not always a previous seller at the place of use, so in those situations 
the contract cannot naturally be returned. 
The sales contract that can be canceled (moving in) can also be canceled when initially notified 
future sales contracts and authorizations, which will be reinstated upon cancellation of move-in 
in connection with.  
In case of contract cancellation, the seller/authorization of the previous/future sales contract 
the party is no longer an active party in the datahub, no sales contract/authorization of course 
be reinstated. If the place of use remains in a state without a contract, a notification will be sent here 
to the distribution system operator.

datahub cannot review the status of previous contracts and restore old contracts 
into effect if necessary, such as in the case of cancellations of contracts introduced through datahub's processes. Provided 
the contract imported in the data conversion must be cancelled, the party informs the datahub operator of this, 
who can perform the cancellation on behalf of the party.

cancellation by the seller. The customer's cancellation can be, for example, based on the customer's right to cancel 
cancellation made or cancellation based on incorrect information provided by the customer. If 
the customer's cancellation concerns the contract announced as move-in, it is possible for the seller to notify 
also that the customer's contract in question is cancelled, but the move-in itself is not cancelled. If 
the contract only, but not moving in, is cancelled, no possible previous sales contract 
be returned to the place of use.

invoicing right/contract information from the beginning of the contract, counting to the period from which the balance settlement window is 
withdrawn. In these cases, datahub cannot automatically restore the previous seller 
contract into force, because despite the cancellation, a period remains from the contract to be canceled, 
during which the said agreement is valid. In this case, datahub will inform the previous seller 
the date from which the seller of the starting contract can notify datahub retroactively, if he wishes 
customer back. AlThe graphs on la show what the customer did before the start of the contract

3.2.5.2 
Cancellation of the online contract 
Cancellation of sales contracts may also lead to cancellation of the online contract. 
The distribution system operator must cancel the network contract in the data hub for its own part, if 
the online contract was originally confirmed based on the canceled sales contract. Cancellation 
based on this, the old network contract is automatically reinstated in datahub if this 
the online contract has been concluded in connection with the creation of the sales contract that can be canceled in datahub.  
In the case of cancellation of the online contract and reinstatement of the old online contract 
similar rules apply to the contractual situation stored in datahub 
in the processing of the sales contract. When the online contract is cancelled, a possible previous one 
the online contract at the place of use is reinstated. If the previous online contract had 
known end date before the contract to be canceled was announced, previous contract 
will be reinstated only up to the respective expiration date. If you have already reached the future 
announces a new online agreement, the previous online agreement can only be reinstated 
until the start of the online contract. If the cancellation is made retroactive to the closing of the balance window 
after cancellation by the customer, the previous online contract does not come back into force, but 
the canceled online contract remains in effect until the closing of the balance window and 
is canceled from then on. If there is no previous online agreement, the place of use remains the online agreement 
when canceling without an online contract. As an exception to the previous one, if the online contract is cancelled 
retroactively due to cancellation of the customer and there is no previous online contract, must be cancelled 
the online contract is canceled only from the moment of notification of cancellation. In this case, it must be cancelled 
the online contract remains valid in datahub from its start date until the moment of notification of cancellation.  
If the contract cancellation notified to datahub is pending notification from the other party 
cancellation, this must be reported no later than seven days later. Later 
notifications of cancellations received are accepted, but for notifications that are repeatedly received late 
will be addressed.

3.2.5.4 
DH-351 and DH-352 Cancellation of termination of contracts 
Terminations of the sales and online contract notified to the contracts can be canceled on their own 
with their events. Termination can be canceled if the termination of the contract has been announced 
into the future and there is no new contract starting at the place of use after the end date.  
Contract terminations introduced in the data conversion cannot be canceled. If in data conversion 
the imported contract is intended to continue despite the announced termination, there is a contract 
to be continued by notifying the place of use of a new contract from the end date onwards.  
3.2.5.5 
Retroactive error correctionthe seeds 
Retrospective changes to the start and end dates of the contracts should only be made in the clear 
in error situations. In retroactive corrections, the main rule is that the balance sheet is determined to have made an error 
according to the seller and contract information according to who should have the right to bill the customer. 
The principle is therefore that the seller who made the mistake is responsible for the balance sheet, even if he has no right 
bill the customer. 
The seller announces the retroactive sales contract with the same announcement as in the future 
of the starting sales contract. The announcement of the new retroactive sales agreement is proceeding as normal 
process, if there are no other vendors' contracts valid for the place of use as indicated 
after the start date of the sales contract. Otherwise, retroactively

3.2.6 
Other contract types 
Datahub will not maintain the background contract models currently in use on the market. 
When such a background contract is activated in the parties' own systems, these will be announced 
as a notification of a new contract in accordance with datahub's contract processes.  
3.2.6.1 
Small production purchase agreements 
For small-scale production sites, a separate use place will be created in the data hub in accordance with current practice and 
start their own separate processes. Small production contracts are treated the same as 
traditional contracts for places of consumption, i.e. there are no differences in the contract processes between small-scale production and 
between consumption locations. As a purchase contract or online service contract for small production 
in datahub, such an agreement is interpreted that is attached to the production location. 
If a production location and a consumption location are combined with a consumption location 
the sales contract is terminated with the reason "emigration", this information is forwarded in addition to the distribution system operator 
also to the seller of the purchase agreement. Combining consumption and production locations makes it possible 
also that when entering into a new contract, the seller is informed by a pre-inquiry about the place of use that 
the location of use is associated with the location of production use. 
3.2.6.2 
Electricity supply contracts 
Electricity supply contracts do not set special requirements for the data hub. In Datahub 
electricity supply contracts are treated as separate sales and network contracts. However, only 
the seller responsible for delivery assigned to the measurement area can notify the electricity supply contract. 
The seller must inform datahub that it is an electricity supply contract, so that 
the distribution system operator knows not to send the contract confirmation of the network contract to the customer when 
receive information about a new contract from datahub. Similarly, when the electricity supply contract 
are converted into separate contracts, the distribution system operator knows based on the same information as the customer 
a separate online contract confirmation must be sent. Information about the electricity supply contract can be 
also used to find out the number and relative share of such contracts. 
The seller who is obligated to deliver has the right to receive information as to whether the customer is covered by the obligation to deliver 
or not in accordance with the delivery obligation limit of Section 21 of the Electricity Market Act. In addition, with a delivery obligation 
the seller has the right to receive information about how much other sellers have in total as energy sum information 
of customers covered by the delivery obligation in the area. Datahub will provide this information 
with a report offered to the seller obliged to deliver via the datahub user interface.

3.3 
DH-200 Measurement data processing 
3.3.1 
Measurement data 
 
FIGURE 363636 CLASS DIAGRAM OF MEASUREMENT DATA 
The figure above shows the data structure of the measurement data. Datahub has three types 
measurement points: places of use, border points and production units (NBS's Production Unit / PU). 
All measurement points are associated with measurement data, but the same measurement time series can only be associated with one 
to the measurement point. All measurement points can also be notified of reactive electricity input and output measurements. 
The place of use cannot have two used for invoicing and balance settlement (reactive power) 
measurement time series. Thus, for example, in items where the consumption of the place of use is formed 
from several measurement time series, only one (sum) time series is reported to the data hub. 
Limit points can have one to four measurement time series, depending on whether electricity can be transferred 
at the border point in both directions and whether the reactive electricity measurement data of the border point is also transmitted. 
Information about which direction electricity can move or whether electricity can move must be assigned to the limit point 
in both directions. Self-use of the production unit is reported to the created for this purpose 
for a consumption site whose subtype is the production unit's own use. For everyone 
a so-called measurement responsibilitythe area that is meant to be in question 
the measurement area managed by the network operator responsible for measuring the border point. Responsible for measurement 
the distribution system operator informs the border point of the energy transferred in different directions (from the area responsible for measurement 
to the parallel area and vice versa) separately with two different active energy measurement time series, and

Datahub can be notified and measurement values ​​can be retrieved from the datahub in the desired unit (Wh, kWh, 
MWh, GWh or varh, kvarh, Mvarh, Gvarh). Measurement data can be delivered to a maximum of 1 Wh 
give or take. For places of use with a fuse size or equivalent electric power of no more than 3x63 A, 
it is recommended to provide measurement data with an accuracy of 1 Wh, the minimum requirement is 10 Wh. 
For applications where the fuse size or the equivalent electric power is greater than 3x63 A, 
the minimum requirement for the accuracy of measurement data is 1 kWh. Reporting of measurement data will 
take into account the above-described accuracies in the number of decimal places in the measurement values. Kilowatt hours 
(kWh), for example, should be reported with at least two and no more than three decimal places at the most 
For 3x63 A applications. When searching for measurement data, you must state in which unit you want the data 
seek.  
The distribution system operator must report the measurement data in the respective statutory and balance sheet 
with the time step used. The Finnish retail market is moving from an hourly measurement to a 15-minute measurement 
to measurement (arm measurement) during the transition period from 1 January 2023 and in the Nordic countries 
from an hourly balance statement to a 15-minute balance statement (quarter balance) from 22 May 2023. Because of this 
datahub will have support for different time steps of measurement data (for example, 15 minutes and 1 
hour). However, measurement data can always be retrieved from the data hub at the desired time step (for example 
15 minutes, hour, month). Datahub returns the measurement data with the time step with which 
the distribution system operator has reported the measurement data to the data hub, if no time has been specified for the search
step. 
Datahub supports the audit-trail function, which means that all changes made to measurement data are saved 
to historical data. 
In the notification of measurement data, the distribution system operator must indicate the time stamp of the measurement data, 
measurement value and measurement data status. In addition to these, datahub maintains the editing time, 
editor and time of receipt information. The editing time is determined based on the time, 
in which case the datahub saves the information in the database. With the editor information, datahub maintains information about which 
process or which user has edited the measurement data at the time of editing. As a rule 
only the distribution system operator can update the measurement data with measurement data notifications. Measurement data 
modified by the datahub operator only at the request of operators in special cases 
in error situations and changed information is forwarded to the parties entitled to the information. Datahub registers 
also separately the recording time of the measurement data, based on which accurate authentication can be done 
afterwards also the moment when the datahub has received the notification of the measurement data. 
Only positive values ​​are processed in Datahub, so for example consumptions and productions 
must always be reported separately. Measurement data is processed according to Finnish official time. Thus 
in connection with clock changes, the length of the day is either 23 or 25 hours.

3.3.2 
DH-210 Notification of measurement data 
The principle is that only new and changed measurement data should be reported to the data hub. 
It is not necessary to report measurement data for entire days. Datahub transmits the measurement data from the same 
for the time period than it has received it. Status is also interpreted as a change in measurement data 
change, even if the measured value remains the same.  
Reporting data to the data hub is generally the responsibility of the person responsible for the measurement of the measurement point. 
Regarding the places of use, the person responsible for measurement is the distribution network operator. The measuring person deviates 
often from the distribution network operator, e.g. for border points, in which case the person in charge of measurement can be 
for example, the network operator. 
3.3.2.1 
Time limits for notification of measurement data 
Time limits measuredfor the notification of rights in the data hub are determined by the message traffic regulation [1] 
in accordance with. Currently, the time limits are defined in this document for the current view 
according to how the time limits will be recorded in the regulation. It should be noted that the datahub 
implementation requires changes to national legislation and the time limits for the balance sheet are yet to be determined 
in this context, to check and, if necessary, update. Weekdays and weekends not separately 
to be taken into account in the time limits of the data hub, which corresponds to the Nordic balance sheet practice. 
Preliminary measurement data for the previous day must be reported to Datahub for the current day 
by midnight. In accordance with the schedule of the upcoming balance sheet of the distribution system operator 
the final measurement data must be reported to datahub by 24:00 on the delivery date 11 days ago 
(EET/EEST) by, after which the balance window for that delivery date closes. 
The next 24 hours will be reserved for Datahub to perform the balance sheet calculations and the data 
for delivery to eSett. In this time, the datahub processes and validates the measurement data, executes 
you calculate and deliver the data to eSett. Enough time should be reserved for these activities so that 
the time limits of the balance sheet can be observed in all situations.

3.3.2.2 
Validation of measurement data 
The responsibility for validating the measurement data and sending the correct measurement data to the data hub is 
with the person in charge of measurement. Datahub performs simple validations for measurement data in those situations 
for which the distribution system operator's validation is not at a sufficient level. Most notably the data hub 
the validation performed by is validation of statuses, the rules of which are described in section 3.3.2.3.  
Datahub performs validation of negative and excessive values ​​depending on the measurement point 
of type. The value is determined to be excessive if the value exceeds ten times the value declared at the place of use 
electric power. Similarly, production capacity is used as a reference value for production units. If 
the electric power of the place of use has not been reported to the datahub, the fuse size must be reported. In this case, datahub 
calculates the electrical power of the place of use from the indicated fuse size.  
Measurement data can be sent with an accuracy of at most 1 Wh, and datahub validates what is allowed 
the number of decimal places depending on the unit used. For example, information can be reported in the kWh unit 
with a maximum of three decimal places.  
Measurement time series data rejected during validation are not stored in the database, but are returned from them 
time series-specific rejection data. The table below lists those performed by datahub 
validations by measurement type.

3.3.2.4 
Control of the notification of measurement data 
Datahub sends reminders to the distribution system operator or the person responsible for the measurement data, if 
the distribution system operator has commissioned this to a 3rd party. Reminders will be sent if above 
the described notification time limits and status handling instructions are not followed. Reminders are sent 
in the event that 
• 
preliminary measurement data for the delivery day (previous day) is not available at the turn of the day 
by at all announced 
• 
Information with missing status has been left unassessed 5 days after delivery or 
• 
after closing the balance window, measurement data with uncertain statuses have remained. 
In the first two cases, reminders are sent once a day until 
measurement data has been corrected or delivered, however for a maximum of 30 days. In the last one 
in this case, the reminder will only go out once, because in some situations it is necessary to leave the uncertain status 
effective also after the closing of the balance sheet settlement window. Uncertain statuses will not be sent, however 
reminders regarding reading measurement items. 
Reminders are sent only after the time limit in question has already been exceeded. In the industry 
should generally be trusted that the distribution system operators follow the agreed rules and build 
the necessary processing for this purpose to their own systems. The purpose of reminders is to point out that 
the rules are not followed. If the distribution system operator does not change based on repeated reminders 
operating methods, we will take a closer look at this operation. Reminders are sent 
only for valid measuring points and places of use to the extent that the place of use 
the online contract is valid. 
In the user interface provided by the datahub, the representatives of the distribution system operators must determine whether they can 
electricity to move at that limit point only in one direction or both. Limit point measurements 
regarding the delivery of measurement data is monitored separately for both transmission directions. If to the limit point 
reporting measurement data for the "wrong" direction, the distribution system operator will be informed of this. 
In addition to the previous reminders, the distribution network operators will be notified if there is an outage 
non-zero values ​​are reported for the place of use. In these cases, the distribution system operator 
the reason for non-zero values ​​must be found and either the measurement data or the state of the place of use must be corrected. 
Reminders are sent once a day until the information is corrected, but no more than 30 
for a day. 
3.3.2.5 
Transmission of measurement data 
All measurement data received by Datahub is automatically forwarded to all parties who 
are entitled to this information. If the distribution system operator has commissioned measurement data 
to the service provider of the notification, the measurement data reported by this can be forwarded 
distribution network operatorunder. Datahub transmits measurement data to one system for each party. If 
the party needs data in several of its own systems, the party provides the measurement data itself

3.3.3 
Handling reading measurements and unmeasured items 
Datahub does not receive or process the readings of reading measurements. The distribution system operator must calculate or 
otherwise, prepare profiles of reading measurements per place of use and report these to the data hub. 
Profiles in Datahub should be created according to the type of user group shown in the current measurement setting 
1 according to the comparison curve. This procedure requires changes to the content of the measurement regulation. 
The profile is created based on the annual usage estimate of the place of use. Currently for type user group 2 
from the use of the calculated so-called balance energy forecast and the associated temperature correction 
we will give up on this. 
Profiles calculated on the basis of the distribution system operator's annual usage estimate are reported to the data hub 
with a status of "Uncertain". The profiles are reported with the status "OK" when the distribution system operator reads 
readings from the meter and based on this, calculates a corrected profile up to the moment of the previous reading. Thus 
the same status rules apply to reading measurements as to other measurements. If the distribution system operator 
corrects the profile indicated with the status "OK", the corrected measurement data must be indicated with the status 
"Fixed-OK". 
There are places of use that do not have energy metering. These are generally used as designations 
unmetered place of use and constant power object. Also for these places of use by the distribution network operator 
measurement data must be reported in time series format. The distribution system operator can prepare an unmetered schedule 
of the profile of the place of use in the desired way, such as by announcing the same energy to each time-
step or by using the comparison curve of type user group 1 mentioned above. Unmeasured 
the status "Evaluated" is used for the measurement data of the place of use, and corrections are made with the status 
"Fixed-OK". 
Profiles and standard power time series of reading measurement objects are reported to the data hub in the same way and 
with the same time limits and validations as other measurement data.  
3.3.4 
Measurement data corrections 
The distribution system operator must correct incorrect measurement data in the data hub for the entire period for which 
measurement data is stored in the data hub (6 years). Corrected measurement data is forwarded to everyone 
to parties entitled to measurement data in accordance with these rights. With this, the parties 
can receive corrected measurement data for the entire time the measurement data is stored in the data hub.

3.3.5 
Processing of parasitic data 
Datahub allows reactive power to be taken from the network - (inductive) and input to the network - (capacitive) 
reporting and searching measurement data for places of use, production units and border points. Parasite electricity 
datahub only acts as an information broker. Therefore, based on the reactive electricity measurement data, no 
calculations are performed in the datahub and data reporting is not monitored. For static electricity measurement data 
only status processing and validation of negative values ​​are carried out, because taking from the network and 
submission to the network must be reported in its own time series. Intermittent power data is not automatically transmitted 
to the seller. An information field is added to the place of use, which says that the place of use is available 
parasitic data. Based on this information, the seller can, if he wishes, order reactive electricity measurement data

3.3.6 
Processing of cut-off point and production unit measurements 
The measurement data of border points and production units is needed in the data hub of the distribution system operator 
to calculate the balance sheet. These measurement data are reported like other measurement data and 
measurement data can also be corrected outside the balance window. Border points and production units 
regarding corrections of measurement data, however, balance errors are not recorded, but possible monetary ones 
corrections are carried out for these directly between the party obliged to measure and this 
between the counterparty (another network operator) one-on-one. 
Corresponding switching status information is used at border points and production units, as at places of use 
is used. Through the user interface, the network company can temporarily remove the border point or 
from the use of the production unit by changing the connection status to the 'under construction' status. Not in this case either 
measurement data must be delivered to these measurement points. 
Reporting the boundary point measurement data to the data hub is the responsibility of the person in charge of the measurement point. 
Thus, for example, the national grid company and regional grid companies must also notify 
border point measurement data to the extent that the balance statement of the second measurement area of ​​the border point is processed 
in datahub. Validation and processing of measurements of limit points and production units is the responsibility of others 
the processing of measurement data as applicable. 
3.3.7 
Netting calculations 
Datahub performs the netting calculation always in connection with the measurement data notification of the distribution system operator. 
The netting of the place of use refers to the interconnected consumption and (small) production places of use 
netting of measurement data within a time step (hour or 15 minutes). In this case, consumption and 
the difference in production (more precisely, its absolute value) is recorded either for consumption or production 
whichever is greater. Parasitic energy is not netted. The table below shows 
example of netting for the first four hours of the day (in the case of hourly measurement).

The netting calculation is based on the data hub's information model on the parallel usage location information 
and to information on the maximum power of the production device of the small production site. The netting calculation is performed 
whenever the parallel usage location information is valid, there is one or more small production usage locations 
production device and the total sum of the maximum output of the production devices is no more than 100 kVA 
(if the conditions for the netting calculation are met, the information "Netting calculation" is stored in the usage location). 
If the total power is more than 100 kVA or the production device has not been declared or the production lawfrom tea 
maximum power information is missing, the place of use is not included in the netting calculation. 
The maximum power of the production device of the small-scale production location is converted in the processing of the data hub 
from the indicated units W, kW, MW, GW directly into units VA, kVA, MVA, GVA. Provided 
the distribution system operator knows of cases where the conversion is not directly available, will 
the distribution system operator changes the power data so that the maximum power is correct after the conversion. 
When the maximum power of the production device changes so that the place of use should either be in the future 
included in the netting calculations or removed from the netting calculations, the distribution system operator must do this 
in connection with the maximum power change, first remove the parallel usage location information from the data hub and 
add the parallel usage location information again after the change. This is how you get the changes 
in relation to the calculations. 
The performance of the calculation does not depend on other information, such as the conditions of the place of use or contracts. 
If one of the pair of usage locations included in the calculation is in "under construction" mode, for that one 
no measurement data is expected for the place of use. The calculation is also performed for both in this case 
for places of use, but the calculation is only made of the measurement data delivered to another place of use 
by. 
The time step of the netting calculation results depends on the time step used in the balance sheet. 
The balance sheet will be carried out with an hourly accuracy until May 2023, when the transition will take place 
in the balance sheet to a 15-minute time step.  
1) When the hourly balance statement is valid, the netting is calculated for the time of the place of use
according to the step. In this case, if hourly metering is valid at the place of use, they are 
netted results at hourly level. Correspondingly, those measured in a 15-minute period 
the netted values ​​of the places of use are calculated with an accuracy of 15 minutes and 
mediated. The distribution system operator of the consumption and production site must ensure, 
that the time step of both places of use corresponds to each other.  
a. Datahub always calculates the netting values ​​for the time of the point of use to be netted
according to the step. Thus, if the time step of the point of consumption is 
for example, an hour and 15 minutes for a production location, calculated by datahub 
the netted values ​​of the place of consumption also with an hourly accuracy and 
the netted values ​​of the production site with an accuracy of 15 minutes. 
Hourly data is divided by four in the netting calculation (see 
example below).  
2) When the balance statement changes to an accuracy of 15 minutes, datahub will calculate 
also the results of the netting always with 15-minute accuracy regardless 
about the measurement accuracy/time step of the places of use.

3.3.8 
Energy community calculations 
Similarly to the netted data, datahub calculates the community energies of the distribution system operator 
in connection with the measurement data notification. As a result, the energy community calculation calculates the consumption
/the so-called of the production use place community energy. Community energy generally refers to the place of use 
consumption or production, from which the share of the place of use has been deducted/added to the community 
from production (depending on whether it is a place of consumption or production use). The energy community can 
specify two different sharing methods: SMA or SMB.

The energy community's calculations are affected by the following information: 
•

of total production

Energy community calculations are performed like netting calculations within a time step (hourly/15 
to the minute). The following general principles apply to calculations: 
• 
The internal netting of the place of use is always calculated before the community calculation 
o The consumption of the netted place of use is deducted in full 
production of a parallel production site

will be transferred as part of the energy community's distributed total production 
o Note this netting principle is also applied in a situation where 
the production location to be netted is assigned to the energy community

into the community's surplus energy 
• 
The results are calculated with the accuracy of the time step of the measurement of the place of use, or 15 
after the introduction of the one-minute balance sheet with an accuracy of 15 minutes 
respectively, as in netting (see chapter 3.3.7). 
Datahub transmits the calculated community energies at the end of the calculation to all those entitled to the information 
parties (distribution system operators, sellers and 3rd parties). Saying tells 
depending on the place of use, whether the time series in question is a time series used in billing or not. 
Market participants can also search for community energy data separately with search events.

3.3.8.1 
Distribution method SMA 
In the SMA distribution method, the surplus energy is recorded in its entirety to the energy community defined 
for (one) production site. 
In addition to the general principles presented above, the following rules are followed in the calculation: 
• 
All surplus energy is recorded for the community defined surplus energy 
to the production site 
o Possible distribution of the consumption place of use and the place of use 
the difference in consumption (production share > consumption) is transferred to surplus energy 
• 
A production site that may belong to the community, which does not belong to the community 
determined surplus energy production location, production (net or 
measured) is transferred in its entirety as part of the shareable by the community 
total production.

3.3.8.2 
SMB distribution method 
In the SMB distribution method, the community's total production is distributed to all consumption sites belonging to the energy community according to these distribution shares. Any surpluses specific to the consumption site are recorded in the parallel production site of the consumption site. In this distribution method, 
the community's surplus energy is only formed for disconnected consumption points. 
The rules for parallel consumption points described below also apply to the so-called virtual consumption point. 
In other words, the normal production point and the virtual production point are treated in the calculations with the same rules. 
The following special rules apply to the calculations of the SMB distribution method: 
• 
The total production of the community is distributed to all consumption points belonging to the energy community in accordance with these percentage distribution shares 
o The share exceeding the consumption of the consumption point (measured or netted) 
is calculated for the parallel production point of the consumption point in question 
o If the consumption point does not have a parallel production point, 
the distribution system operator must establish a so-called virtual 
utility (see chapter 3.1.4) 
• 
The share of the disconnected consumption point is transferred to the 
surplus energy production point assigned to the community 
Community energies are thus calculated for different types of consumption points as follows:

3.4 
DH-400 Connection and disconnection processes 
3.4.1 
Overview 
From Datahub's perspective, connections and disconnections are changes in the status of the usage point, which are 
reported separately in connection with the contract processes and during delivery in connection with the parties' 
collection processes or modification work performed at the usage point.in. Datahub forwards the seller's requests 
to the distribution system operator about the change in status of the place of use, as well as information about the change in status 
from the distribution system operator to the seller. 
The time limits for connecting and disconnecting requests are determined by which part of the overall process 
the procedure is performed. When connecting or disconnecting takes place as part of the moving process, not separately 
disconnection or connection request, but the distribution system operator connects or disconnects the point of use 
electricity as needed at the end of the contract processes, when the time limits for information exchange are determined 
in accordance with contract processes. Thus, for example, in situations of moving, the connection to the place of use can 
be possible to receive under certain conditions for the current day (more detailed description in the contract processes). 
The operating model for reconnection is specific to the network company. It is always indicated in the connection request 
the connection's contact person and his/her phone number, so that the distribution system operator can ensure a safe connection 
connection. 
The seller must make cut-off requests related to collection processes no later than a week before 
the desired day. When the customer pays the bill to be collected, one should strive for good customer service 
for the fastest possible reconnection. If the customer pays the invoice before requested 
cut-off date, the cancellation of the cut-off request must be notified with a separate cancellation notice. If 
the customer pays the bill on the requested cut-off date, the seller must inform the place of use 
connection request. This is how it works, because the distribution system operator may not be able to cancel 
disconnection only on the same day when the electricity disconnection is to be carried out. Datahub cares 
the seller's connection request in real time to the distribution network operator, who processes it for the cut-off date 
the incoming connection request according to its own processes. If the distribution system operator still has time to cancel 
based on the connection request made on the day of the disconnection, the distribution system operator must respond 
to the seller's original disconnection request with a disconnection notice, where the status of the place of use is 
specified as "connected". In addition to this, the distribution system operator must respond to the seller's connection request 
respectively. Otherwise, the distribution system operator must notify the performed disconnection 
according to the basic process. The procedure described above ensures that the original 
the disconnection request can be processed to the end in all situations, and the datahub will not be left waiting 
disconnection notice from the distribution system operator, if the disconnection is not carried out.  
The distribution network operator may not connect the point of use before the seller's connection request, if there is a disconnection 
made accordingly at the seller's request. If the seller needs to inform the distribution system operator that 
electricity in a place of use that is already switched off must not be switched on, the seller must also 
in this case indicates a request to disconnect the access point. The distribution system operator must respond to this request 
with a new cut-off notice for the actual cut-off date, even if it is for your own needs 
already notified the datahub of the completed disconnection.

When the distribution system operator's connection or disconnection notice is used to change the one under construction 
connected or disconnected as the status of the point of use, the distribution system operator must first remember to update 
the property information for the respective location of use, if it was previously missing. Datahub does not allow 
connection or disconnection of the place of use, if any mandatory information about the characteristics of the place of use 
is missing. 
By default, the distribution system operator reports the connection or disconnection as soon as the information is available 
available in the distribution system operator's own system, i.e. like any other 
updating the location information. In the case of an item where connection or disconnection is performed 
manually, can update the information to the system of the distribution network and through it to the data hub 
a delay that is allowed to be a maximum of one week. Delays of more than a week for connection and disconnection requests 
answering will be monitored by the datahub operator. Cut-off and 
connection requests are not validated based on status information in the datahub, as it may be from here 
due to the delay, your current one is incorrect. The seller can always send connection or disconnection requests 
according to datahub status information. The distribution system operator has the correct status information, when 
the distribution system operator is able to process the seller's requests correctly in its own processes. 
As an example of the method of operation, a situation where the seller has first requested disconnection due to debt collection, and 
the distribution system operator will manually cut off the electricity at the point of use on the morning of the request day. Customer 
informs the seller that he has paid the bill as soon as the electricity goes out, but the seller cannot see the data hub 
proper state of place of use because verseThe distribution network operator does not yet have the information in its own system due to a manual disconnection. Even if the point of use is currently connected in Datahub, the seller can 
send a connection request to Datahub, which the distribution network operator can forward to the installer. 
If the distribution network operator is unable or unwilling to connect the point of use in accordance with the seller's request, 
the distribution network operator will notify this with a connection delay event no later than the weekday following the requested 
connection or disconnection date. Delays longer than this in responding to requests will be monitored by the datahub operator. The event explanation can 
provide the reason why the connection cannot be made. If necessary, this delay notification can be notified 
several times. If the distribution network operator is unable to implement the requested disconnection on the date requested by the seller, the electricity delivered to the point of use must be included in the distribution network operator's 
balance. The distribution system operator must notify the seller of this delay via datahub. 
If necessary, the seller can request connection on a new day. The previous connection request is cancelled based on the new request. The electricity supply at the point of use is again included in the seller's balance from the moment the distribution system operator connects the electricity to the point of use based on the seller's connection request. However, if the connection is reported late outside the balance window for one reason or another, the electricity consumed at the point of use may be included in the losses of the metering area for the period outside the balance window. The distribution system operator may not always be able to estimate the correct day for connection or disconnection. If necessary, the distribution system operator may report a delay in connection or disconnection several times using the same event. 
The distribution system operator usually charges a fee for connections and disconnections performed on a short schedule, outside working hours or without remote connection. In these 
cases, the distribution system operator invoices the seller or the customer, depending on which party has requested the connection or disconnection. 
The distribution system operators' price lists have been compiled in a standard table on the datahub 
service portal so that the seller can easily provide additional information on the costs of connections and disconnections

3.5 
DH-500 Distribution System Operator's Imbalance Settlement 
This chapterthe distribution system operator's balance sheet calculations performed in the vataa data hub as well as 
notifications of balance sheet information to eSett and the parties. After commissioning, datahub handles 
balance settlement reporting to eSett on behalf of the distribution system operator with regard to all data. Ad hoc 
a user interface is also created for datahub, so-called for the maintenance of structural data in respect of those data, 
for which there are no separate messaging processes. Datahub forwards to the distribution system operator 
information about the balance deviations of the measurement areas calculated by eSett and the confirmed limit point sums.  
The distribution system operator is responsible for the calculations of the balance settlement information described in this chapter 
reporting data to datahub in accordance with the agreed rules and time limits. Datahub 
is responsible for performing the balance sheet calculations and forwarding these to eSett in the Nordics 
following the rules of the balance sheet settlement model (NBS). The rules of the NBS model are described in eSett 
in the manual published by [4]. From Datahub, balance sheet information can also be searched for this information 
by authorized parties.  
The diagram below shows the daily balance settlement process, with the most important tasks 
are performing balance sheet calculations based on structural data and measurement data and 
information exchange of balance sheet information. Balance sheet calculations depend on DH-120, DH-200, DH-300 and DH-
400 processes and maintaining the structural information of the balance sheet through the user interface. 
The information to be processed in the balance sheet and exchanged between the parties is described in more detail 
later in this chapter.
